#################### CRIANDO UMA NOVA TABELA DENTRO DO MYSQL CONTÉM APENAS 2 CAMPOS
#################### TABELA TITLES É A BASE PARA CRIAÇÃO DA NOVA TABELA cp_titles_date_2 COM OS CAMPOS TITLE E TO_DATE

mysql> create table cp_titles_date_2 select title, to_date from titles;
Query OK, 443308 rows affected (15.42 sec)
Records: 443308  Duplicates: 0  Warnings: 0

mysql> select * from CP_titles_date_2 limit 10;
+-----------------+------------+
| title           | to_date    |
+-----------------+------------+

| Senior Engineer | 9999-01-01 |
| Senior Staff    | 9999-01-01 |
| Staff           | 1996-02-11 |
+-----------------+------------+
10 rows in set (0.00 sec)


################### ATUALIZANDO OS REGISTROS DO Staff para NULL na COLUNA TO_DATE

mysql> update cp_titles_date_2 set to_date=NULL where title='Staff';
Query OK, 107391 rows affected (3.43 sec)
Rows matched: 107391  Changed: 107391  Warnings: 0
